          • B.4 Lane 4 — Negative results / replication / critique ($0–$2k)

          • B.7 Lane 7 — FM-aided wet-lab / clinical application ($5k–$50k)

          • B.9 Lane 9 — FM-aided experimental design / active learning ($1k–$10k FM-side) — new 2026
